  <script>
    // Auto-hide error message after 5 seconds (KECUALI jika locked)
    const err = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
    const isLocked = <%= typeof locked !== 'undefined' && locked ? 'true' : 'false' %>;
    
    if (err && err.style.display !== 'none' && !isLocked) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        err.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease, transform 0.5s ease';
        err.style.opacity = '0';
        err.style.transform = 'translateY(-10px)';
        setTimeout(() => {
          err.style.display = 'none';
        }, 500);
      }, 5000);
    }

    // ===== TAMBAHAN: Toggle show/hide password =====
    const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('togglePasswordBtn');
    const passwordInput = document.getElementById('password');

    if (toggleBtn && passwordInput) {
      toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        const isPassword = passwordInput.type === 'password';
        passwordInput.type = isPassword ? 'text' : 'password';
        this.classList.toggle('is-visible', isPassword);
        this.setAttribute('aria-label', isPassword ? 'Sembunyikan password' : 'Tampilkan password');
        this.setAttribute('aria-pressed', isPassword ? 'true' : 'false');
        passwordInput.focus();
      });

      toggleBtn.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
          e.preventDefault();
          this.click();
        }
      });
    }

    // Loading state on form submit
    const form = document.getElementById('loginForm');
    const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
    
    form.addEventListener('submit', function() {
      btn.innerHTML = `
        <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" style="animation: spin 1s linear infinite;">
          <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-opacity="0.25"></circle>
          <path d="M12 2a10 10 0 0 1 10 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round"></path>
        </svg>
        <span>Memproses...</span>
      `;
      btn.style.opacity = '0.8';
      btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
      btn.disabled = true;
    });

    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.innerHTML = `@keyframes spin { 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }`;
    document.head.appendChild(style);

    if (err && err.style.display !== 'none' && !isLocked) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        err.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
      }, 100);
    }

    // ✅ COUNTDOWN TIMER & LOCK FORM
    <% if (typeof locked !== 'undefined' && locked) { %>
    (function() {
      let seconds = <%= typeof retryAfter !== 'undefined' ? retryAfter : 900 %>;
      const timeLeftEl = document.getElementById('timeLeft');
      const errorMsg = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
      const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
      const emailInput = document.getElementById('email');
      const passInput = document.getElementById('password');
      const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('togglePasswordBtn');
      
      // 1. Disable form & tombol login
      if (submitBtn) {
        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        submitBtn.style.opacity = '0.5';
        submitBtn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
        submitBtn.innerHTML = `
          <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
            <rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2" ry="2"></rect>
            <path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0 1 10 0v4"></path>
          </svg>
          <span>Akun Dikunci</span>
        `;
      }
      
      if (emailInput) emailInput.disabled = true;
      if (passInput) passInput.disabled = true;
      if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.style.display = 'none';

      // 2. Fungsi update timer setiap detik
      function updateTimer() {
        if (seconds <= 0) {
          clearInterval(timerInterval);
          // Sembunyikan error & buka kembali form
          if (errorMsg) {
            errorMsg.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease';
            errorMsg.style.opacity = '0';
            setTimeout(() => { errorMsg.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
          }
          if (submitBtn) {
            submitBtn.disabled = false;
            submitBtn.style.opacity = '1';
            submitBtn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
            submitBtn.innerHTML = `
              <span>Masuk ke Sistem</span>
              <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">
                <line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"></line>
                <polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"></polyline>
              </svg>
            `;
          }
          if (emailInput) {
            emailInput.disabled = false;
            emailInput.focus();
          }
          if (passInput) passInput.disabled = false;
          if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.style.display = 'flex';
          
          // Optional: reload halaman setelah unlock
          setTimeout(() => { window.location.reload(); }, 1000);
          return;
        }
        
        const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
        const secs = seconds % 60;
        if (timeLeftEl) {
          timeLeftEl.textContent = `${mins.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${secs.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
        }
        seconds--;
      }

      // 3. Jalankan timer
      updateTimer();
      const timerInterval = setInterval(updateTimer, 1000);
    })();
    <% } %>
  </script>
</body>
</html>

        const stats = { aktif: 0, akanBerakhir: 0, segeraBerakhir: 0, expired: 0 };
        if (mitra && mitra.length > 0) {
          mitra.forEach(m => {
            if (m.badgeClass === 'active') stats.aktif++;
            else if (m.badgeClass === 'warning') stats.akanBerakhir++;
            else if (m.badgeClass === 'danger') stats.segeraBerakhir++;
            else if (m.badgeClass === 'expired') stats.expired++;
          });
        }
      %>

              <th onclick="sortTable(4)">Berakhir</th>
              <th onclick="sortTable(5)">Sisa Hari</th>
              <th onclick="sortTable(6)">Status</th>

              <th>Aksi</th>

            <% if (mitra && mitra.length > 0) { %>
              <% mitra.forEach(m => { %>
                <%
                  // 🔒 LOGIKA AKSES: Cek apakah user boleh edit mitra ini
                  const isHumas = user?.role === 'humas';
                  const isAdminFakultas = user?.role === 'admin_fakultas';
                  const isGuest = user?.role === 'guest';
                  
                  // Admin fakultas boleh edit HANYA jika fakultas_id cocok
                  const isOwnFaculty = isAdminFakultas && 
                    user.fakultas_id && 
                    m.fakultas_id &&
                    user.fakultas_id.toLowerCase().trim() === m.fakultas_id.toLowerCase().trim();
                  
                  // Humas bisa semua, Admin Fakultas hanya milik fakultasnya
                  const canEdit = isHumas || isOwnFaculty;
                %>
                
                <tr>
                  <td data-label="Kode">
                    <span class="kode-mitra"><%= m.kode_mitra %></span>
                    <br><strong style="display:none" class="mobile_instansi"><%= m.nama_instansi %></strong>
                  </td>
                  <td data-label="Instansi"><strong><%= m.nama_instansi %></strong></td>
                  <td data-label="Kontak" class="contact-cell">
                    <strong><%= m.nama_kontak || '-' %></strong>
                    <% if (m.no_hp_kontak) { %>
                      <small>📞 <a href="tel:<%= m.no_hp_kontak %>"><%= m.no_hp_kontak %></a></small>
                    <% } %>
                  </td>
                  <td data-label="Email">
                    <% if (m.email_fakultas) { %>
                      <a href="mailto:<%= m.email_fakultas %>" class="email-link"><%= m.email_fakultas %></a>
                    <% } else { %>
                      <span style="color: var(--text-muted)">-</span>
                    <% } %>

                    <%= m.sisa_hari %>
                  </td>

                    <span class="status-badge status-<%= m.badgeClass %>"><%= m.status %></span>
                  </td>

  <script>
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
  console.log('🚀 Page loaded completely');
  
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  const table = document.getElementById('mitraTable');
  const resultCount = document.getElementById('resultCount');
  
  if (!searchInput) {
    console.error('❌ searchInput tidak ditemukan!');
    return;
  }
  
  if (!table) {
    console.error('❌ table tidak ditemukan!');
    return;
  }
  
  const dataRows = [];
  const allTr = table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
  allTr.forEach(tr => {
    if (!tr.querySelector('.empty-state')) {
      dataRows.push(tr);
    }
  });
  
  console.log(`✅ Found ${dataRows.length} data rows`);
  
  function updateStats() {
    let aktif = 0, warning = 0, danger = 0, expired = 0;
    
    dataRows.forEach(row => {
      if (row.classList.contains('hidden-row')) return;
      
      const badge = row.querySelector('.status-badge');
      if (!badge) return;
      
      if (badge.classList.contains('status-active')) aktif++;
      else if (badge.classList.contains('status-warning')) warning++;
      else if (badge.classList.contains('status-danger')) danger++;
      else if (badge.classList.contains('status-expired')) expired++;
    });
    
    const elAktif = document.getElementById('statActive');
    const elWarning = document.getElementById('statWarning');
    const elDanger = document.getElementById('statCritical');
    const elExpired = document.getElementById('statExpired');
    
    if (elAktif) elAktif.textContent = aktif;
    if (elWarning) elWarning.textContent = warning;
    if (elDanger) elDanger.textContent = danger;
    if (elExpired) elExpired.textContent = expired;
    
    console.log(`📊 Stats: ${aktif} aktif, ${warning} warning, ${danger} danger, ${expired} expired`);
  }
  
  searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
    const keyword = this.value.toLowerCase().trim();
    let visibleCount = 0;
    
    console.log(`🔍 Search: "${keyword}"`);
    
    dataRows.forEach(row => {
      const text = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
      
      if (keyword === '' || text.includes(keyword)) {
        row.classList.remove('hidden-row');
        visibleCount++;
      } else {
        row.classList.add('hidden-row');
      }
    });
    
    if (resultCount) {
      resultCount.textContent = `${visibleCount} mitra ditemukan`;
    }
    
    updateStats();
  });
  
  console.log('✅ Search ready - try typing something!');
  
    
    // ✅ TAMBAHKAN JUGA: Handler resize biar konsisten
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
        sidebar.classList.remove('active');
      } else {
        sidebar.classList.remove('hidden');
        mainWrapper.classList.remove('expanded');
        sidebarToggle.classList.remove('shifted');
      }
    });
  }
  
  window.sortTable = function(colIndex) {
    const tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
    const rows = Array.from(tbody.querySelectorAll('tr')).filter(r => r.querySelector('td'));
    
    rows.sort((a, b) => {
      const aText = a.cells[colIndex]?.textContent.trim() || '';
      const bText = b.cells[colIndex]?.textContent.trim() || '';
      return aText.localeCompare(bText);
    });
    
    rows.forEach(row => tbody.appendChild(row));
  };
  
  window.exportTable = function() {
    let csv = 'Kode,Instansi,Kontak,Email,Status\n';
    dataRows.forEach(row => {
      if (row.classList.contains('hidden-row')) return;
      const cells = row.querySelectorAll('td');
      csv += `"${cells[0]?.textContent.trim()}","${cells[1]?.textContent.trim()}","${cells[2]?.textContent.trim()}","${cells[3]?.textContent.trim()}","${cells[6]?.textContent.trim()}"\n`;
    });
    
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = 'mitra.csv';
    a.click();
  };
});
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  <script>
    // ========== URL GAS WEB APP ==========
    let GAS_WEB_APP_ALERT;
    fetch('/api/gas-url')
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(data => { GAS_WEB_APP_ALERT = data.url; })
      .catch(err => console.error('Gagal load GAS URL:', err));
      
    <!-- // ========== SIDEBAR TOGGLE ========== -->
    <!-- const sidebarToggle = document.getElementById('sidebarToggle'); -->
    <!-- const sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar'); -->
    <!-- const mainWrapper = document.querySelector('.main-wrapper'); -->

    <!-- if (sidebarToggle && sidebar) { -->
      <!-- sidebarToggle.addEventListener('click', () => { -->
        <!-- if (window.innerWidth <= 768) { -->
          <!-- sidebar.classList.toggle('active'); -->
          <!-- sidebarToggle.classList.toggle('shifted'); -->
        <!-- } else { -->
          <!-- sidebar.classList.toggle('hidden'); -->
          <!-- mainWrapper.classList.toggle('expanded'); -->
          <!-- sidebarToggle.classList.toggle('shifted'); -->
        <!-- } -->
      <!-- }); -->

      <!-- window.addEventListener('resize', () => { -->
        <!-- if (window.innerWidth > 768) { -->
          <!-- sidebar.classList.remove('active'); -->
        <!-- } else { -->
          <!-- sidebar.classList.remove('hidden'); -->
          <!-- mainWrapper.classList.remove('expanded'); -->
          <!-- sidebarToggle.classList.remove('shifted'); -->
        <!-- } -->
      <!-- }); -->
    <!-- } -->

    // ========== KIRIM EMAIL VIA GAS ==========
    let countdownInterval;

    async function sendTestEmail(button) {
      const mitraId = button.dataset.mitraId;
      const mitraName = button.dataset.mitraName;
      const mitraEmail = button.dataset.mitraEmail;           // email_fakultas (penanggung jawab)
      const mitraEmailAsli = button.dataset.mitraEmailAsli;   // email_mitra_asli (referensi)
      const sisaHari = button.dataset.sisaHari;

      // Validasi: email penanggung jawab wajib ada
      if (!mitraEmail) {
        showModal({
          success: false,
          title: 'Data Tidak Lengkap',
          message: 'Email Penanggung Jawab (Fakultas) belum diisi. Silakan lengkapi data mitra terlebih dahulu.',
          data: null
        });
        return;
      }

      // Disable button & tampilkan loading
      button.disabled = true;
      button.classList.add('sending');

      try {
        // ⚠️ PENTING: Tidak menggunakan headers 'Content-Type: application/json'
        // karena akan memicu CORS preflight yang ditolak oleh Google Apps Script
        const response = await fetch(GAS_WEB_APP_ALERT, {
          method: 'POST',
          body: JSON.stringify({
            mitra_id: mitraId,
            nama_instansi: mitraName,
            email_fakultas: mitraEmail,         // Penerima email (wajib)
            email_mitra_asli: mitraEmailAsli,   // Info referensi (opsional)
            sisa_hari: sisaHari
          }),
          redirect: 'follow' // Wajib agar browser mengikuti redirect otentikasi GAS
        });

        const result = await response.json();

        if (result.success) {
          // Ubah tombol jadi hijau "Terkirim"
          button.classList.remove('sending');
          button.classList.add('sent');
          button.innerHTML = '✅ Terkirim via GAS';
          
          // Tampilkan modal sukses
          showModal({
            success: true,
            title: 'Email Berhasil Dikirim via GAS!',
            message: `Notifikasi peringatan telah dikirim ke Email Penanggung Jawab. Silakan cek inbox (atau folder spam) dalam beberapa menit.`,
            data: {
              email_pj: result.data.email,
              email_mitra: mitraEmailAsli || null,
              nama_instansi: result.data.nama_instansi,
              sisa_hari: result.data.sisa_hari
            }
          });
        } else {
          button.classList.remove('sending');
          button.disabled = false;
          button.innerHTML = '🔄 Coba Lagi';
          
          showModal({
            success: false,
            title: 'Gagal Mengirim Email',
            message: result.message || 'Terjadi kesalahan saat mengirim email via GAS.',
            data: null
          });
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Error:', err);
        button.classList.remove('sending');
        button.disabled = false;
        button.innerHTML = '🔄 Coba Lagi';
        
        showModal({
          success: false,
          title: 'Koneksi ke GAS Gagal',
          message: 'Tidak dapat terhubung ke Google Apps Script. Pastikan URL Web App sudah benar dan deployment aktif.',
          data: null
        });
      }
    }

    // ========== MODAL FUNCTIONS ==========
    function showModal({ success, title, message, data }) {
      const modal = document.getElementById('resultModal');
      const modalBox = document.getElementById('modalBox');
      const icon = document.getElementById('modalIcon');
      const titleEl = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
      const messageEl = document.getElementById('modalMessage');
      const detailEl = document.getElementById('modalDetail');
      const countdownText = document.getElementById('countdownText');

      // Reset class
      modalBox.classList.remove('success', 'error');
      icon.classList.remove('success', 'error');
      titleEl.classList.remove('success', 'error');

      if (success) {
        modalBox.classList.add('success');
        icon.classList.add('success');
        titleEl.classList.add('success');
        icon.textContent = '✅';
        
        if (data) {
          // Email Penanggung Jawab (wajib)
          document.getElementById('detailEmailPJ').textContent = data.email_pj || '-';
          
          // Email Mitra (opsional - tampilkan hanya jika ada)
          const emailMitraRow = document.getElementById('detailEmailMitraRow');
          if (data.email_mitra) {
            document.getElementById('detailEmailMitra').textContent = data.email_mitra;
            emailMitraRow.style.display = 'flex';
          } else {
            emailMitraRow.style.display = 'none';
          }
          
          document.getElementById('detailInstansi').textContent = data.nama_instansi || '-';
          document.getElementById('detailSisaHari').textContent = (data.sisa_hari || 0) + ' hari';
          detailEl.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
          detailEl.style.display = 'none';
        }
        countdownText.style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        modalBox.classList.add('error');
        icon.classList.add('error');
        titleEl.classList.add('error');
        icon.textContent = '❌';
        detailEl.style.display = 'none';
        countdownText.style.display = 'none';
      }

      titleEl.textContent = title;
      messageEl.textContent = message;
      modal.classList.add('show');

      // Auto close setelah 5 detik (hanya untuk sukses)
      if (success) {
        startCountdown(5);
      }
    }

    function closeModal() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('resultModal');
      modal.classList.remove('show');
      if (countdownInterval) {
        clearInterval(countdownInterval);
      }
    }

    function startCountdown(seconds) {
      const countdownEl = document.getElementById('countdown');
      let remaining = seconds;
      countdownEl.textContent = remaining;

      if (countdownInterval) clearInterval(countdownInterval);
      
      countdownInterval = setInterval(() => {
        remaining--;
        countdownEl.textContent = remaining;
        if (remaining <= 0) {
          clearInterval(countdownInterval);
          closeModal();
        }
      }, 1000);
    }

    // Tutup modal saat klik di luar
    document.getElementById('resultModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      if (e.target === this) closeModal();
    });

    // Tutup modal dengan ESC
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal();
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>

                                                    class="btn btn-sm <%= u.is_active ? 'btn-danger' : 'btn-success' %>"
                                                    onclick="openModal(
                                                        '<%= u.id %>', 
                                                        '<%= u.name || u.email.split('@')[0] %>', 
                                                        '<%= u.email %>', 
                                                        <%= u.is_active %>
                                                    )">

            <div class="table-footer">

                <span>💡 Gunakan search untuk mencari user tertentu</span>
            </div>

    <script>
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
  console.log('🚀 Page loaded completely');
  
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  const table = document.getElementById('userTable');
  const resultCount = document.getElementById('resultCount');
  
  if (!searchInput) {
    console.error('❌ searchInput tidak ditemukan!');
    return;
  }
  
  if (!table) {
    console.error('❌ table tidak ditemukan!');
    return;
  }
  
  const dataRows = [];
  const allTr = table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
  allTr.forEach(tr => {
    if (!tr.querySelector('.empty-state')) {
      dataRows.push(tr);
    }
  });
  
  console.log(`✅ Found ${dataRows.length} data rows`);
  
  function updateStats() {
    let humas = 0, admin = 0, guest = 0;
    
    dataRows.forEach(row => {
      if (row.classList.contains('hidden-row')) return;
      
      const badge = row.querySelector('.role-badge');
      if (!badge) return;
      
      if (badge.classList.contains('role-humas')) humas++;
      else if (badge.classList.contains('role-admin')) admin++;
      else if (badge.classList.contains('role-guest')) guest++;
    });
    
    const elHumas = document.getElementById('statHumas');
    const elAdmin = document.getElementById('statAdmin');
    const elGuest = document.getElementById('statGuest');
    
    if (elHumas) elHumas.textContent = humas;
    if (elAdmin) elAdmin.textContent = admin;
    if (elGuest) elGuest.textContent = guest;
    
    console.log(`📊 Stats: ${humas} humas, ${admin} admin, ${guest} guest`);
  }
  
  searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
    const keyword = this.value.toLowerCase().trim();
    let visibleCount = 0;
    
    console.log(`🔍 Search: "${keyword}"`);
    
    dataRows.forEach(row => {
      const text = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
      
      if (keyword === '' || text.includes(keyword)) {
        row.classList.remove('hidden-row');
        visibleCount++;
      } else {
        row.classList.add('hidden-row');
      }
    });
    
    if (resultCount) {
      resultCount.textContent = `${visibleCount} user ditemukan`;
    }
    
    updateStats();
  });
  
  console.log('✅ Search ready - try typing something!');
  
  
  // Modal Functions
  window.openModal = function(userId, userName, userEmail, isCurrentlyActive) {
    const modal = document.getElementById('confirmModal');
    const icon = document.getElementById('modalIcon');
    const title = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
    const message = document.getElementById('modalMessage');
    const nameEl = document.getElementById('modalUserName');
    const emailEl = document.getElementById('modalUserEmail');
    const form = document.getElementById('confirmForm');
    const submitBtn = document.getElementById('modalSubmitBtn');
    
    nameEl.textContent = userName;
    emailEl.textContent = userEmail;
    
    if (isCurrentlyActive) {
      icon.className = 'modal-icon danger';
      icon.textContent = '🚫';
      title.textContent = 'Nonaktifkan User?';
      message.textContent = 'User yang dinonaktifkan tidak bisa login ke sistem sampai diaktifkan kembali.';
      submitBtn.className = 'btn btn-danger';
      submitBtn.textContent = '🚫 Nonaktifkan';
    } else {
      icon.className = 'modal-icon success';
      icon.textContent = '✅';
      title.textContent = 'Aktifkan User?';
      message.textContent = 'User akan bisa login kembali ke sistem setelah diaktifkan.';
      submitBtn.className = 'btn btn-success';
      submitBtn.textContent = '✅ Aktifkan';
    }
    
    form.action = `/users/${userId}/toggle-status`;
    form.style.display = 'block';
    modal.classList.add('show');
  };
  
  window.closeModal = function() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('confirmModal');
    modal.classList.remove('show');
  };
  
  document.getElementById('confirmModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeModal();
  });
  
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal();
  });
  
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
      e.preventDefault();
      searchInput.focus();
      searchInput.select();
    }
  });
  
  updateStats();
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>

  </div>
</aside>

<!-- ✅ SCRIPT SIDEBAR TOGGLE (GLOBAL - JALAN DI SEMUA HALAMAN) -->
<script>
(function() {
  'use strict';
  
  function initSidebar() {
    const toggle = document.getElementById('sidebarToggle');
    const sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar');
    const mainWrapper = document.querySelector('.main-wrapper');
    
    if (!toggle || !sidebar) return;

    // Cegah duplikasi listener jika script ter-load 2x
    if (toggle.dataset.initialized === 'true') return;
    toggle.dataset.initialized = 'true';

    function handleToggle() {
      if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
        sidebar.classList.toggle('active');
      } else {
        sidebar.classList.toggle('hidden');
        if (mainWrapper) mainWrapper.classList.toggle('expanded');
      }
      toggle.classList.toggle('shifted');
    }

    function handleResize() {
      if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
        sidebar.classList.remove('active');
      } else {
        sidebar.classList.remove('hidden');
        if (mainWrapper) mainWrapper.classList.remove('expanded');
      }
      toggle.classList.remove('shifted');
    }

    toggle.addEventListener('click', handleToggle);
    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
    console.log('✅ Sidebar toggle initialized globally');
  }

  // Jalankan segera jika DOM sudah ready, atau tunggu DOMContentLoaded
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initSidebar);
  } else {
    initSidebar();
  }
})();
</script>
